We arrived in Modesto from Dallas late. This bar sits surrounded by a motel (Tiki Motel). We thought about staying at the motel, then walking over to bar- lol- my husband goes to the motel window, presents his Texas ID, and the motel manager says, ‚Äúyou don‚Äôt wanna stay here or any motel on McHenry. There‚Äôs lots of drugs, we do family relocation, and the police are here all the time.‚Äù He suggested places out on Hwy 99- which we did find! Thank you!

After in our hotel we went back to the bar. We had been traveling all day and needed a few drinks before calling it a night.

We parked out back. Parking is tiny. Based upon our prior research- this is the ‚Äúbest gay bar‚Äù in Modesto. It looked kinda ‚Äúdive bar‚Äù- but we do ‚Äúdive bar well‚Äù

First in you are ‚Äúhard carded‚Äù for ID- then metal detector run over you. That‚Äôs wild! Only in REALLY BAD dive bars have we ever seen this.

We took a seat at the bar. The chairs/stools are something right outta  ‚ÄúPier one imports‚Äú - the padding‚Äôs on the bar edges terribly worn out. The seating in back is red and worn- inside is TINY! This place is small!

We had a few drinks and crowd began to pickup. Most seemed like your typical ‚ÄúJr college rural‚Äù crowd. The bar is definitely ‚Äúdive bar quality‚Äù. If this is ‚Äúthe best in Modesto‚Äù- I‚Äôm terrified at what the other looks like.

There were some local  street ‚Äúurchins‚Äù from the tiki hotel wandering around- so I guess the metal detector makes sense. This is a rough part of town it seems- based upon our observations and what we were told.

Drinks were on par with most bars in price and quality- we left before midnight as to not risk being in the area to long.</review>

< text>
One of the cheapest high quality gas stations in the area - as evidenced by the constant lines that are at least 4 deep at all hours of the day. They recently started accepting credit cards! Long hoses allow filling up from either side of the vehicle. An attendant is available during regular business hours to help and will pump gas for those that have disabilities. I think the lines have been a little shorter since they remodeled the lot and put in the Quick Quack, but it's difficult to determine the long-term effects.</text>
